## 收获祭2

lang="zh"><div class="poem">许多村民们聚集在村外的农田，发生什么事了？——秋静叶<br>与【<a href="./大家的幻想乡-人物-秋静叶.md" title="大家的幻想乡/人物/秋静叶">秋静叶</a>】一同前往【<a class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">当秋静叶快要接近农田时，传来的只有人们的哀嚎与痛哭。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭2-10" ## 收获祭3

<table><tbody><tr class="tt-status-header" id="收获祭3-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,1&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-status" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,30&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">嗯，不过快了。来，把你手上的文稿和相机给我。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭3-31" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,31&#93;"><td id="射命丸文" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">射命丸文</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">这可是大新闻啊！你不可以抹杀一名记者揭露真相的权利！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭3-32" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,32&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">想吃阴阳玉吗？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭3-33" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,33&#93;"><td id="射命丸文" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">射命丸文</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">好啦好啦……给你，别动粗就好……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-narrator" id="收获祭3-34" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,34&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-narrator" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">东西到手后，灵梦迅速将秋静叶的照片删除。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭3-35" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,35&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">你别在这唯恐天下不乱了，那两只烤红薯的神明是不可能搞出这种破坏的，一定有人在暗中利用她们！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭3-36" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,36&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">稿子就还给你了，做一只聪明的天狗，幻想乡需要和平。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭3-37" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,37&#93;"><td id="射命丸文" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">射命丸文</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">知道啦，清廉正直的我，可不会做那种昧着良心博人眼球的事情~</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭3-38" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,38&#93;"><td id="射命丸文" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">射命丸文</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">但文文新闻的发布工作是不能停止的，我也只能给你们稍微多留出一点调查真相的时间。你们明白的吧？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭3-39" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,39&#93;"><td id="射命丸文" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">射命丸文</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">另外，最近天狗村落经常有物品丢失……你们有什么头绪么？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭3-40" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,40&#93;"><td id="射命丸文" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">射命丸文</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">说完，文文就溜走了。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-status-header" id="收获祭3-42" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d3&quot;,42&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem">完成委托<br>获得【<a href="/%E5%A4%A7%E5%AE%B6%E7%9A%84%E5%B9%BB%E6%83%B3%E4%B9%A1/%E7%89%A9%E5%93%81/%E6%AD%A6%E5%99%A8#天狗的玩具相机" title="大家的幻想乡/物品/武器">天狗的玩具相机</a>】<br></div></td></tr></tbody></table>



## 收获祭4

<table><tbody><tr class="tt-status-header" id="收获祭4-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d4&quot;,1&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem">目前状况紧急，只能与灵梦、魔理沙分头行动了，希望可以赶得及找到那对神明姐妹。<br>前往【<a href="/index.php?title=%E5%A4%A7%E5%AE%B6%E7%9A%84%E5%B9%BB%E6%83%B3%E4%B9%A1/%E5%9C%B0%E5%9B%BE/%E8%BF%B7%E9%80%94%E7%AB%B9%E6%9E%97&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" class="poem">玩家</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">按照那位记者小姐的说法，我们的时间已经不多了。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭4-3" class="poem">无论是收获祭，还是关于秋静叶小姐的流言传播……下一期报纸出版的时间可是迫在眉睫了!</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭4-4" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d4&quot;,4&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" title="大家的幻想乡/物品/道具">上海人偶</a>】</div></td></tr></tbody></table>



## 收获祭7

data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d9&quot;,20&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-narrator" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">文文新闻：受重伤的秋静叶突然出现在博丽神社？！怠惰的博丽巫女破天荒的勤奋工作？！……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭9-21" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d9&quot;,21&#93;"><td id="玩家" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">玩家</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">怎么回事？！难道灵梦小姐她真的退治了秋静叶小姐？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭9-22" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d9&quot;,22&#93;"><td id="稗田阿求" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">稗田阿求</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">不要慌张。你看，文文的措辞极其模糊，说明她们也不知道究竟是谁做的。灵梦应该还在寻找真相甚至还在找帮手……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭9-23" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d9&quot;,23&#93;"><td id="稗田阿求" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">稗田阿求</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">不对不对，这不是现在要考虑的。你快去神社，不然……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-narrator" id="收获祭9-24" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d9&quot;,24&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-narrator" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">外面突然变得嘈杂起来。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭9-25" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d9&quot;,25&#93;"><td id="村民" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">村民</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">快去神社把凶手抓起来！</div></td></tr></tbody></table>

class="poem">上一次人间之里发生这种规模的动乱是什么时候呢？</div></td></tr></tbody></table>



## 收获祭10

class="poem">……快，我们回一趟人间之里！现在村落很危险！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-status-header" id="收获祭10-142" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d10&quot;,142&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem">完成委托<br>获得【<a href="/%E5%A4%A7%E5%AE%B6%E7%9A%84%E5%B9%BB%E6%83%B3%E4%B9%A1/%E7%89%A9%E5%93%81/%E9%98%B2%E5%85%B7#天狗面具" title="大家的幻想乡/物品/防具">天狗面具</a>】</div></td></tr></tbody></table>



## 收获祭11

## 收获祭12

<table><tbody><tr class="tt-status-header" id="收获祭12-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d12&quot;,1&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-status" class="poem">完成委托</div></td></tr></tbody></table>

## 收获祭14

## 收获祭16

<table><tbody><tr class="tt-status-header" id="收获祭16-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d16&quot;,1&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem">小铃也被天邪鬼迷惑了吗……狡猾的家伙，这次一定要抓住你！——博丽灵梦<br>与【<a href="./大家的幻想乡-人物-博丽灵梦.md" title="大家的幻想乡/人物/博丽灵梦">博丽灵梦</a>】一同前往【<a href="/index.php?title=%E5%A4%A7%E5%AE%B6%E7%9A%84%E5%B9%BB%E6%83%B3%E4%B9%A1/%E5%9C%B0%E5%9B%BE/%E9%9B%BE%E4%B9%8B%E6%B9%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">怎么会？那笨蛋该不会这个时候跑出去了吧！现在情况这么混乱，就不要再擅自给我增加麻烦啊！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭16-8" ## 收获祭17

<table><tbody><tr class="tt-status-header" id="收获祭17-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d17&quot;,1&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-status" ## 收获祭18

<table><tbody><tr class="tt-status-header" id="收获祭18-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,1&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem">真是一波未平一波又起，这种生来就是为了煽动人心的妖怪实在太讨厌了！——博丽灵梦<br>与【<a href="./大家的幻想乡-人物-博丽灵梦.md" title="大家的幻想乡/人物/博丽灵梦">博丽灵梦</a>】一同击败【<a href="/index.php?title=%E5%A4%A7%E5%AE%B6%E7%9A%84%E5%B9%BB%E6%83%B3%E4%B9%A1/%E5%9C%B0%E5%9B%BE/%E5%A6%96%E6%80%AA%E4%B9%8B%E5%B1%B1&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="大家的幻想乡/地图/妖怪之山（页面不存在）" unred="">秋穰子（困难）</a>】</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-narrator" id="收获祭18-2" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,2&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-narrator" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,70&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-narrator" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">人间之里，收获祭。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-narrator" id="收获祭18-71" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,71&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-narrator" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">村民们乱作一团，而天邪鬼快意地看着这一切。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭18-72" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,72&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">这是怎么回事！跟班，灵梦去哪了？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-narrator" id="收获祭18-73" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,73&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-narrator" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">听到动静匆匆赶来的魔理沙被眼前的乱象吓了一跳，但是没有人能顾得上回答她。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭18-74" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,74&#93;"><td id="鬼人正邪" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">鬼人正邪</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">嘿，这样就行了，接下来的事情就麻烦你们咯~黑白的魔法使！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭18-75" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,75&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">你这家伙，究竟是怎么逃出来的？！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭18-76" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,76&#93;"><td id="鬼人正邪" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">鬼人正邪</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">幸好你们的绳子不是那么结实呢，可是我还是忍着放弃了第一时间逃跑的机会，就是为了在这种时候完成逆转！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭18-77" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,77&#93;"><td id="鬼人正邪" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">鬼人正邪</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">那么，再见啦，你们就继续慢慢收拾这个残破的局面吧！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭18-78" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,78&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">可恶！跟班！你悄悄跟上那个天邪鬼，这些村民暂且交给我来处理！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭18-79" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d18&quot;,79&#93;"><td id="玩家" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">玩家</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">好的！</div></td></tr><tr class="poem">……</div></td></tr></tbody></table>

id="男人" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">男人</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽神社的巫女小姐吗？请以后不要再让这个孩子去做这么危险的事情了啊……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭19-46" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d19&quot;,46&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">呃，对……对不起……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭19-47" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d19&quot;,47&#93;"><td id="男人" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">男人</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">话说，这个就是罪魁祸首吗？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-narrator" id="收获祭19-48" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d19&quot;,48&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-narrator" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">长相酷似周杰伦的村民指了指被自己扛在肩上仍然昏迷的天邪鬼。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭19-49" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d19&quot;,49&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">是啊，就是她，造成了这一连串的事件……不，被称之为灾难也不为过吧……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="收获祭19-50" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d19&quot;,50&#93;"><td id="抗鬱薬おじさん" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">抗鬱薬おじさん</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">就把她交给我吧，我回村子里把消息带给大家。那么这里就拜托你了，巫女小姐。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-narrator" id="收获祭19-51" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d19&quot;,51&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-narrator" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">……</div></td></tr></tbody></table>



## 收获祭20

<table><tbody><tr class="tt-status-header" id="收获祭20-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;\u6536\u83b7\u796d20&quot;,1&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem">一切都结束了呢。真好。<br>使用【<a href="./大家的幻想乡-人物-秋静叶.md" title="大家的幻想乡/人物/秋静叶">秋静叶</a>】举行一场【大型宴会】</div></td></tr></tbody></table>
